[\[1b.1\]{D1516}]@##/_/rgya gar skad du/_shrA TA kAr+Na ba ta n+h+ra maN+Tal tsa kra Sh+ya sA d+ha nar t+na pad+ma rA ga ni d+hi nA ma/_bod skad du/_dpal mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo'i sgrub thabs pad+ma rA ga'i
[\[1b.2\]]gter zhes bya ba/_dpal bcom ldan 'das mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho la phyag 'tshal lo/_/gang zhig sangs rgyas thams cad kyi/_/thugs rjes kun bsdus ngo bo'i sku/_/dngos grub gcig bsdus rang bzhin
[\[1b.3\]]te/_/rgyud kyi phyag can lhan skyes zhal/_/gnyis med shes rab phag mo dang /_/lhan cig bzhugs pa de la 'dud/_/mkhyen pa'i gsung gi 'od zer gyis/_/snod ldan blo mun sel mdzad cing /_/
[\[1b.4\]]don gyi bdud rtsis tshim mdzad ba/_/mtsho skyes la sogs bla ma'i tshogs/_/zla ba lta bu rnams la 'dud/_/dpal ldan mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho yi/_/bla ma'i man ngag mngon rtogs rim/_/ji bzhin rtogs
[\[1b.5\]]pa'i nus med kyang /_/bdag nyid dran phyir bri bar bya/_/de la thog mar dpal mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i dpar bskur ba'i rim pas dag par byas pa zab pa dang rgya che ba la lhag par mos pas rgyud kyi don khong du chud

[\[2a.1\]]pa'i sgrub pa pos/_skye bo med pa'i sa phyogs dang /_ri bo dang /_ri'i phug dang /_bya skyibs dang /_rgya mtsho chen po'i 'gram dang /_gdod ma nas grub pa'i dur khrod dang /_gang du yid dga' ba'i gnas su yang rung ste/_bcom ldan 'das kyi
[\[2a.2\]]ras ris dang /_gtor ma dang /_mchod yon la sogs pa'i nye bar spyod pa rnams dang ldan pa'i bsam gtan gyi gnas bstar ba/_bdud rtsis gtor zhing /_me tog gcal du bkram pas dga' bar byas par/_tho rengs sad pa dang rdo rje rnal 'byor ma
[\[2a.3\]]rnams kyis glu dang cang te'u'i sgras bskul bar bsams te/_gdong gi gtsang sbra la sogs byas nas/_ro dngos kyi steng ngam mi'i pags pa la sna tshogs rdo rje bris pa'i steng du/_gcer bu khar bdud rtsi'i ri lu bcug pa lhor mngon par
[\[2a.4\]]phyogs pas/_rdo rje'i skyil krung la sogs pas 'dug ste/_lag pa g.yon pa'i dbus dang mthe'u chung nas bzung ba'i sor mo rnams kyi rtsa ba la/_dpal mo'i go cha rnams kyis sbyang ba dang /_bcom ldan 'das kyi go cha yang dbus dang sor mo

[\[2b\]]
[\[2b.1\]]nyid kyi mthe bong dang srin lag sbyar bas chang gtor te yan lag lnga la khrus dang /_mthor 'thung dang /_mchod pa'i rdzas rnams la bsang gtor yang bya'o/_/de nas rang gi mdun du chang de nyid dang /_dri zhim po bsres pas maN+Dal gru bzhi par byugs te me tog sil
[\[2b.2\]]mas gtor la rdo rje phyag rgyas reg cing b+hur b+hu wa swaHzhes brjod pas sa 'og dang /_sa steng dang /_mtho ris kyi rang bzhin du byin gyis brlab bo/_/de nas oM AHs+thA nAM mer k+Sha hUM zhes brjod cing me tog gcig rang gi 'og tu bzhag bas gnas bsrung bar bya'o/_/a AHa+wat+mA nA me
[\[2b.3\]]rak+Sha hUM zhes bya ba dang /_me tog gcig rang gi mgo bor bzhag ste bdag nyid bsrung bar bya'o/_/'khyud pa'i phyag rgya dang oM AHyo gAM mer k+Sha hUM zhes bya bas rnal 'byor bsrung bar bya'o/_/de'i rjes su sems can 'khor ba sdug bsngal gyi rgya mtshor bying ba rnams phyag rgya chen po'i go 'phang
[\[2b.4\]]la gzhag pa'i phyir bdag gis dpal mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho bsgom par bya'o zhes sems bskyed do/_/de nas tha mal pa'i lus nyid la/_dpa' bo'i go cha'i sngags brjod cing gnas de dang der rdo rje'i phyag rgya reg bas go cha bya'o/_/de nas me tog dang bcas pa'i thal mo sbyar la
[\[2b.5\]]dpal ldan rdo rje mkha' 'gro ni/_/mkha' 'gro ma yi 'khor los sgyur/_/ye shes lnga dang sku gsum ste/_/'gro ba skyob la phyag 'tshal lo/_/ji snyed rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma/_/rnam par rtog pa'i 'ching gcod cing /_/'jig rten bya ba rab 'jug ma/_/de snyed rnams la rtag phyag 'tshal/_/srid pa'i
[\[2b.6\]]rgya mtshor yongs bying ba/_/yang dag yongs su sgrol mkhas ba'i/_/bla ma dam pa'i drin gang gis/_/bdag la ye shes 'di skyed 'dud/_/cis bya bas mkha' 'gro dang /_mkha' 'gro ma rnams dang /_dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnams yid kyis gsal bar byas la me tog gtor zhing

[\[3a.1\]]paM yongs su gyur pa las sna tshogs pad+ma 'dab ma brgyad pa/_de'i steng du ra~M yongs su gyur pa las nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor dang /_de'i steng du yi ge hU~M kha dog nag po ye shes lnga'i rang bzhin 'od zer kha dog sna tshogs 'phro bzhin pa bsams la/_ngag tu thog mar oM

[\[3a.3\]]lha'i tshogs rim bzhin du stod dang /_bar dang /_smad rnams las gzugs med pa dang gzugs dang 'dod pa'i khams kyi ris rnams spros te khams gsum gyi bgegs rnams med par byas nas/_rang rang gi gnas su bsdu ba ni/_ngag dug par byed pa'o/_/de nas spyi bo dang /_

[\[3b.1\]]bya ba ni yid dag par byed pa'o/_/de nas phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams lha'i nga rgyal bsgom par bya'o/_/de nas gzugs kyi phung po ni rnam par snang mdzad do/_/tshor ba'i phung po ni rdo rje nyi ma'o/_'du shes kyi phung po ni pad+ma gar gyi dbang phyug go/_/'du byed kyi phung po ni rdo rje
[\[3b.2\]]rgyal bo'o/_/rnams par shes pa'i phung po ni rdo rje sems dpa'o/_/de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag nyid ni shrI he ru ka rdo rje'o/_/mig dag ni gti mug rdo rje'o/_/nyan pa dag ni zhe sdang rdo rje'o/_/sna dang ni phrag dog rdo rje'o/_/kha dag ni 'dod chags rdo rje'o/_/

[\[3b.4\]]rnams kyang slob dpon shes rab bsrungs kyis bkod pa bzhin du rtogs par bya'o/_/de nas g.yon pa'i mdzub mo dang mthe bong brdabs pa sngon du 'gro bas/_oM suM b+ha ni suM b+ha kA yi kaM hUM hUM phaT/_oM gr-ih+Na gr-ih+Na bA tsiM kAM hUM hUM phaT/_oM gr-ih+NA pa ya gr-ih+NA pa ya tsi tA kaM tsa ra si maM
[\[3b.5\]]hUM hUM phaT/_oM A na ya hoHb+ha ga wAn badzra ni kaM hUM hUM phaT ces bya ba brjod pas snying ga'i hUM las kha dog nag po dang /_ljang gu dang /_dmar po dang /_ser po'i mdog can rnams te tshangs pa'i mtha' nas 'og gser gyi sa gzhi la thug gi bar du sngags kyi gzugs chen po shar
[\[3b.6\]]dang byang dang nub dang lho'i phyogs rnams su kha phyir phyogs pa rim pas spros pa dgod par bya'o/_/de nas rang gi 'og char ram yongs su gyur pa las nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor la hUM sngon po yongs su gyur pa las sna tshogs rdo rje shin tu chen po gser gyi sa gzhi la thug pa/_hUM gis

[\[4a.1\]]gur dang bla re yang bsam par bya'o/_/de nas suMb+ha la sogs pa'i sngags bzhi las grub pa'i kha'i gdong can ma la sogs pa'i lha mo bzhi dang /_oM dang hUM hUM phaT las grub pa'i gshin rje brtan ma la sogs pa bzhi bo rnams zhal gcig phyag gnyis ma

[\[4a.3\]]kyi tshogs rnams ra ba'i phyi rol du bkug pa'i dbus brgyad du/_hUM phyogs skyong gi kha dog dang mthun pa bsams te bgegs kyi tshogs rnams hUM la bsdus la/_de rnams gyur pa las phyogs skyong brgyad du bskyed par bya'o/_/de nas hUM gi sgra drag la ring ba bsgrags pas/_de
[\[4a.4\]]rnams rang rang gi mdun du me'i dong chen po dmigs te lha mo rnams kyis de rnams su bcug ste phur bus mgo bo nas gdab cing /_oM g+ha g+ha g+ha ta ya g+hA ta ya sarba duSh+TA na phaT/_kI la ya kI la ya sa rba pA paM phaT hUM hUM hUM badzra d+ha ra a dz+nyA pa ya ti bi g+haM kA ya bA katsi t+ta dzra kI
[\[4a.5\]]la ya hUM phaT/_ces bya ba lan gsum brjod pas mgrin pa dang snying gar yang gdab po/_/de nas oM badzra mung+ga ra badzra badzra kI lA ko Ta ya hUM phaT ces bya ba lan gsum brjod pas rdo rje tho bas brdungs te rnam par rtog pa dang bcas pa'i srog dang bral nas gnyis su med pa'i ye shes

[\[4a.7\]]kun nas bgegs dang bral ba'o zhes nga rgyal bya'o/_de nas snying ga'i sa bon las spros pa'i 'od zer rnams kyis/_bla ma dang /_dpal mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i dkyil 'khor spyan drangs te sngar gyi maN+Dal gyi dbus su bzhugs par bya'o/_/de nas oM AHhUM zhes lan gsum brjod

[\[4b.4\]]pa'i chang dbul bar bya'o/_/kun mkhyen ye shes phung po can/_/'gro don rab tu sgrub pa po/_/yid bzhin nor bu 'dir byung ba dang /_dpal sdom khyod la phyag 'tshal lo/_/sna tshogs yi shes chen pos g.yogs/_thams cad bdag nyid rtug tu bzhugs/_thugs rjes khro ba
[\[4b.5\]]drag chen po/_dpal sdom khyod la phyag 'tshal lo/_/zhes bya bus bstod par bya'o/_/bgyis dang bgyid stsal rjes su yi rangs la sogs sdig pa ma lus pa ni skyon rnams ma lus nges par bcom pa yis/_/mdun du so so bshags bya slar la yang ni mi byed pa yi
[\[4b.6\]]sdom gzung ba nyid du bya/_/nyan thos dang ni bse ru bla med rgyal ba rgyal dang rgyal ba'i sras kyis bsags pa'i dge ba la/_/rjes su yi ni rang zhing chub yang dag yongs su bsngo bar bdag gis bya/_/rgyal ba rin chen la sogs gsum la ji snyed skyabs su 'gro bar bya ba

[\[5a.1\]]shAn+ya swa b+hA wa shUn+yo ny+rahaM/_o~M sarbad+harmaHswa b+hA wa shu ng+d+ho \u0f85haM/_oM shU n+ya tA dz+nyA na badzra swa b+hA wa A t+ma ko\u0f85haM/_oM yong shud+d+haH sarba d+harmA yog shud+d+ho\u0f85haM/_zhes bya ba brjod cing don dran par byas te chos thams cad nam mkha'i dkyil ltar bsgom par
[\[5a.2\]]bya'o/_/de nas sngon gyi smon lam gyis sad pa'i sems nam mkha' la nA da la rim gyis rdzogs pa'i hUM blta'o/_/de dang dus mnyam du bsrung ba'i rab la sogs pa rnams kyang blta bar bya'o/_/de'i nang gi 'og gi char yaM sngon po yongs su gyur pa las rlung gi dkyil 'khor sngon
[\[5a.3\]]po gzhu'i dbyibs lta bu mtha' gnyis na g.yo bzhin pa'i ba dan yaM gis byin gyis brlab bo/_/de'i steng du raM dmar po yongs su gyur pa las me'i dkyil 'khor dmar po gru gsum pa 'bar ba bzhin pa'i grwa can raM yig gis byin gyis brlabs pa'o/_/de'i steng bu baM dkar po yongs
[\[5a.4\]]su gyur pa las chu'i dkyil 'khor dkar po zlum po bum pa dang bcas pa la baM yig go/_/de'i steng du laM ser po yongs su gyur pa las/_sa'i dkyil 'khor ser po gru bzhi pa grwar rdo rje rtse gsum pa dang ldan pa laM yig gis byin gyis brlabs pa'o/_/de'i steng du yi ge suM kha dog sna
[\[5a.5\]]tshogs pa yongs su gyur pa las rin po che bzhi'i rang bzhin gyi ri rab zur bzhi ba rtse mo brgyad dang ldan pa suM yig gis byin gyis brlabs pa'o/_/de'i steng du baM yongs su gyur pa las sna tshogs pad+ma de'i steng du hUM yongs su gyur pa las sna tshogs rdo rje bsams te/_/'byung ba rnams
[\[5a.6\]]zhu zhing sla ba'i rang bzhin du gyur nas gcig du 'dres pas ri rab 'og tu ltung bas 'byung ba zhu ba'i gong bu sna tshogs rdo rje'i steng du chags pa yongs su gyur pa las/_gzhal med khang sgo rim pa bzhi dang ldan pa ste/_dbus su ni chos kyi 'byung gnas gru gsum pa'i nang du'o/_/
[\[5a.7\]]gnyis pa gru bzhi pa la/_/gsum pa grwa lnga pa dang /_bzhi par zur drug pa'i nang du ste/_mdog dmar po steng du bltas pa rnams so/_/dkyil 'khor gsum ni zlum po yin la kun gyi phyi ma ni gru bzhi ba ste/_kun kyang gzhal yas khang gi rgyan thams cad dang ldan pa dur khrod dang

[\[5b.1\]]bcas pa'o/_/dkyil 'khor nang ma ni g.yas g.yon gnyis kyi rlung gnyis dbu mar 'jus pa'i rang bzhin gnag pa dang /_/sngo ba'i rtsig pa gnyis pa'o/_/gnyis pa ni sku gsung thugs dag pa'i rang bzhin sngo ba dang dmar po dang dkar bo'i rtsig pa gsum dang ldan pa'o/_/
[\[5b.2\]]gsum pa ni dga' ba bzhi dag pa'i rang bzhin sngon po dang ser po dang dmar po dang ljang gu'i ri mo bzhi dang ldan pa'o/_/kun gyi phyi rol ni ye shes lnga dag pa ste phyi rol du dkar po dang bcas pa'o/_/kun gyi dkyil 'khor dbus ma'i dbus su sna tshogs pad+ma 'dab ma bzhi bcu rtsa brgyad pa/_
[\[5b.3\]]lte ba la nyi ma'i steng du 'jigs byed chen po dang dus kyi mtshan mo'o/_/de'i phyi rol du 'khor lo rim pa gsum pa dang ldan pa/_/de'i phyi rol bskal pa bzang po'i snam bu dang bcas pa'o/_/phyi ma rnams la yang dus kyi pad+ma ma gtogs pa'o/_/pad+ma'i phyi rol nas nang gi phyi ma'i
[\[5b.4\]]'khor lo'i bar gyi mtshams rnams kyi phreng ba ni/_rim pa bzhin du gri gug dang rin po che dang rdo rje dang pad+ma dang 'khor lo dang ral gri dang sna tshogs rdo rje dang thod pa dang mgo bo dang keng rus dang zhags pa dang lcags kyu'i phreng ba rnams kyis bskor ba'o/_/'khor lo'i rtsibs
[\[5b.5\]]rnams ni sum cu rtsa drug go/_/'khor lo'i rtsibs re re'i steng du'ang ro'i gdan re re'o/_/de bzhin du pad+ma'i 'dab ma lha'i gnas rnams dang sgo dang mtshams rnams su yang ngo /_/lha'i gnas ma yin pa mtshams kyi pad+ma rnams la ni rin po che'i bum pa re re'o/_/'khor lo'i
[\[5b.6\]]kha dog rnams ni 'chad par 'gyur te/_de ltar rten gyi dkyil 'khor dmigs te rgyas par ni 'chad par 'gyur ba rnams kyis kyang shes par bya'o/_/de nas 'jigs byed dang dus mtshan gyi steng gi chang A li nyis 'gyur g.yon skor las de'i gzugs brnyan dang ldan pa'i zla ba

[\[6a.1\]]cad re'i bdag nyid can du byas nas 'dus te de nyid du zhugs pas rdo rje sngon po rtse lnga ba/_lte ba la hUM gis byin gyis brlabs pa ni so sor rtog pa'i rang bzhin no/_/hUM las kyang 'od zer sna tshogs dpag tu med pa byung ste sngar lha nyid du bsgrubs pa ma lus pa
[\[6a.2\]]dang gdod ma nas grub pa thams cad bkug ste/_de nyid du gzhug pa 'di ni bya ba grub pa'o/_/de rnams thams cad yongs su gyur pa las rgyu'i he ru ka bskyed ba ni chos kyi dbyings shin tu rnam par dag pa'i ngo bo ste de yang /_skya mdog dkar po zhal bzhi ba/_/spyan gsum
[\[6a.3\]]phyag ni bcu gnyis pa/_/shes rab kha sbyor sbyor bdag nyid/_/byis pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa'o/_/dkar dang ljang gu dmar po dang /_/ser po g.yon nas bskor ba'o/_/zhal gyi ral pa'i cod pan la/_/sna tshogs rdo rje zla phyed 'dzin/_/'phrog byed dka' mo mnyam par
[\[6a.4\]]mnan/_/g.yas brkyang zhabs kyis yang dag bzhugs/_/rdo rje dril bu glang chen gyi/_/bags pa cang te'u gri gug dang /_/dgra sta rtse gsum de bzhin du/_/kha T+waM ga snod zhags pa dang /_/mgo ste g.yon dang g.yas par ro/_/shes rab rang dang 'dra ba la/_/'on
[\[6a.5\]]kyang bud med mtshan nyid ldan/_/de nas de nyid kyi thugs kar nyi ma la gnas pa'i hUM gi sa bon blta bar bya ste 'di ni bsnyen pa'o/_/de nas yab kyi gsang ba'i rdo rje mi dmigs pa las hUM sngon po las rdo rje sngon po rtse lnga ba'o/_/yi ge byaM dmar ser las nor bu ste de nyid kyis

[\[6b.1\]]dang snying gar bkod la tsum+ba na zhes bya'o/_/de nas yi ge gsum brjod cing dga' ba brtsam par bya ste/_/snying ga'i sa bon 'od zer dang rdo rje dang pad+ma'i dga' ba'i sgras phyogs bcu'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad bskul te/_/zhal du zhugs nas lha mo'i pad+mar babs

[\[6b.3\]]'thon te rang rang gi gnas su pad+ma'i 'dab ma rnams la 'dug nas bskul bar mdzad pa ste/_de yang mkha' 'gro ma la sogs pa drug gis mgrin gcig tu/_/mnga' bdag nyi ma re rer 'gro ba mgron 'bod na/_/khyod ni ci yi phyir na stong pa nyid du bzhugs/_/bzhengs shig bzhengs

[\[10b.4\]]dang /_skyon rab tu zhi ba dang /_bdud rtsi 'chang dang /_mi'i zla ba dang /_shin tu gzigs dang /_rab tu brgyan pa dang /_nor bu'i 'od dang /_ri bo brtsegs pa'i tog dang /_don nges ldan dang /_tshe sbyin dang /_rin chen 'byung gnas dang /_skye dbang mtshungs dang /_

[\[15a\]]
[\[15a.1\]]zhes bya ba ni 'khor lo gsum pa'i dkyil 'khor la rim pa gnyis dang bcas pa'o//_//de nas phyi rol slar yang 'dir/_/me yi 'khor lo bdag gis bshad/_/kha dog dmar po 'bar chen po/_/sum cu drug rtsibs rnams mchog la/_/rnal 'byor
[\[15a.2\]]ma slar dgod bya ba/_/lha sogs rigs las byung ma ste/_/lha mo klu mo gnod sbyin mo/_/'byung po ngo bo tsam po'o/_/de kun gsungs pa 'di ni ci/_/lha yi rigs 'byung bshad par bya/_/ma dang chung ma sring mo dang /_bu mo sring mo'i bu mo dang /_/pha yi sring mo de dang ni/_/zhang
[\[15a.3\]]po yi ni chung ma dang /_/chung ma'i spun zla ma dang ni/_/chung ma yi ni ma dang ni/_/de nyid kyi ni pha yi ma/_/chung ma yi ni phyi mo dang /_/ma yi ma dang gnyen mo dang /_ma yi spun zla'i bu mo dang /_/rang gi phyi mo'i spun zla dang /_/spun zla'i bu mo de'i bu mo/_/pha yi ma dang phyi mo dang /_/khu
[\[15a.4\]]bo yi ni chung ma dang /_/bu mo'i bu yi chung ma dang /_/slar yang chung ma'i spun zla dang /_/rang pha'i sring mo'i bu mo dang /_/de nyid kyi ni rang rigs skyes/_/spun zla'i chung ma bu mo dang /_/bu nyid kyi ni bu mo dang /_/bu de yi ni chung ma dang /_/bu mo'i khyo yi ma yi ni/_/bu nyid kyi ni sgyug mo
[\[15a.5\]]dang /_/bu mo'i bu mor yang dag bshad/_/pho nya sum cu drug rnams so/_/kha dog dmar por yang dag grags/_/mtshon cha la sogs sngar dang mtshungs/_/sa ni ring du spong nyid dang /_/dgra bo'i gling du gnas pa mo/_/'du bar rtag tu shes bya ste/_/shes rab thabs bdag ngo
[\[15a.6\]]bo can/_/nus pa'i 'khor lor 'dir rtag tu/_/shes bya rang 'dra'i mdzes pa mo/_/kun du rdo rje'i phreng la sogs/_/lugs 'byung lugs las bzlog pa yis/_/g.yon dang g.yas pa'i lag pa yis/_/'dir ni mchod pa byed pa yin/_/phyugs rnams kyi ni sha thams
[\[15a.7\]]cad/_/kun du son nas dbul bar bya/_/btung ba rnam pa sna tshogs dbul/_/bldag bya sna tshogs nyid de bzhin/_/rang rang stan las langs nas ni/_/bla ma rdo rje 'dzin pa mchod/_/slar yang 'ongs nas 'khor lo yi/_/mchod pa bcu gnyis rnams la'o/_/zhes bya ba ni longs
[\[15b\]]
[\[15b.1\]]rdzogs pa'i me'i 'khor lo ste dang po'o//_//de nas de yi phyi rol bshad/_/chu yi 'khor lo rdzu 'phrul che/_/mdog dkar sum cu drug rtsibs gsal/_/rnal 'byor ma ni rim pas bsgom/_/ma ka ra mo ru sbal nya/_/sbal mo rus sbal chu sram mo/_/sdig nag gag+gir ma shi lAM ma/_/
[\[15b.2\]]chu yi phug ma srin bu'i gdong ma dang /_/cha gab mo kaN TI mo sU yI mo/_/chu byi mo dang grog mo'i gdong ma dang /_/chu yi mi mo dang ni rgod ma dang /_/glang chen mo dang stag mo ce spyang mo/_/chu sbrul mo dang dud mo 'gron bu mo/_/nya phyis ma dang nor bu dzi gu rim dang /_/lI sI mo dang dud
[\[15b.3\]]ngu rim kar+No Ta/_/pha Ta ka mo dA ba kA ma kri mI mo/_/dzu ShI mdang sha sbrang ka lA ma/_/lha yi gtso mo mchog rnams so/_/de ltar kha dog rang bzhin ni/_/dkar mo'am rang rigs skyes pa'o/_/gdong pa rang rang gzugs kyis te/_/rnal 'byor ma'i rim ji bzhin no/_/nye ba'i
[\[15b.4\]]'du ba nyid dang ni/_/sa ni mi g.yo ba mchog go/_/'dzam bu'i gling du gnas par ni/_/shes bya mtshon cha sngon bzhin no/_/yang na gang ba'i rigs sogs kyis/_/mi rnams sum cu drug blta'o/_/gnas sogs rim pa de rnams su/_/mi mo dngos su yang dag bya/_/'dzam
[\[15b.5\]]bu gling 'di de yis ni/_/dum bu bcu gnyis kyis brgyan pa'o/_/ba tsha zhes bya'i rgya mtsho ni/_/de ru gtogs pa'i skye bo rnams/_/drod gsher skyes dang 'du 'phrod las/_/skyes pa mngal nas skyes par bsam/_/'khor lo 'di ni drod gsher skyes/_/me yi 'khor lo mngal
[\[15b.6\]]skyes so/_/mtshan nyid thams cad yongs rdzogs pa'i/_/shes rab thabs nyid rang ngo /_/zhes bya ba ni chu'i 'khor lo ste gnyis pa'o//_//de nas de yi phyi rol 'chad/_/kun nas ye shes 'khor lo'o/_/sum cu drug rtsibs sna tshogs mdog_/lha min mo'i
[\[15b.7\]]rigs rim pa dang /_/til mchog ma dang phul du bde/_/lha yi bu mo dga' chen mo/_/dga' dang dgar grags bde chen ma/_/dung can sna tshogs glang chen ma/_/gzugs chen mo dang gzugs mdzes ma/_/'dod chags rnams rnam sgeg bde ba mo/_/me tog 'dod ma ut+pal
[\[16a\]]
[\[16a.1\]]dkar/_/ut+pal sngo dang mdzes ma dang /_/'dod chags ma dang 'dod chags che/_/rol grags ma dang rol chen ma/_/myos ma dang ni myos dga' ma/_/'dod pa mo dang 'dod chen mo/_/bde las byung dang bde ldan ma/_/mthun mchog ma dang
[\[16a.2\]]byams pa mo/_/skal bzangs ldan ma skal bzangs mo/_/dma' ba mo dang zhum pa mo/_/skyes gzugs mar ni grags pa ste/_/rnal 'byor ma yi gtso mo mchog_/thams cad shes rab thabs bdag nyid/_/rnam pa sna tshogs mdog de bzhin/_/phyag dang mtshon cha sngon bzhin
[\[16a.3\]]shes/_/legs pa'i blo gros de bzhin/_/dur khrod rin po cher sna dang /_/rang byung bde ba byed pa po/_/de phyir longs spyod rdzogs sku'o/_/de nas de yi phyi rol du/_/zla gdugs dang /_'od 'phro ba dang /_dri med rgyal po dang /_ye shes grags pa dang /_kun du rgyal ba dang /_
[\[16a.4\]]yon tan 'od dang /_sgra grags dang /_zla ba rgyas pa dang /_pad+ma'i 'od zer dang /_brtul zhugs bzang po dang /_sgron ma'i rgyal po dang /_glog gi tog dang /_'od zer rgyal po dang /_skar mkhan dang /_grags pa rdzogs ldan dang /_pad+ma'i snying po dang /_rgyal dang /_spyan mdzes
[\[16a.5\]]dang /_rnyog pa med pa'i don dang /_drag shul bde ba dang /_bsod nams gzi brjid dang /_mthu rtsal can dang /_thogs pa med pa'i blo dang /_sgra gcan lha dang /_ye shes dung po dang /_kha lo sgyur dang /_skye dbang mtshungs dang /_me tog gi tog dang /_sgra gcan 'dzin
[\[16a.6\]]dang /_sman chen po dang /_rgyu skar rgyal po dang /_sman pa'i rgyal po dang /_bsod nams glang po dang /_gcod par mdzad pa dang /_rnam par grags pa'i rgyal po dang /_nyi ma'i 'od zer dang /_chos kyi mdzod dang /_blo gros bzang po dang /_yon tan dbang mtshungs dang /_rdo rje'i
[\[16a.7\]]sde dang /_shes rab brtsegs dang /_legs par gnas pa dang /_blo sbyangs dang /_tshangs pa'i dbyangs dang /_yon tan mchog dang /_'brug sgra dbyangs dang /_mngon par shes pa'i tog dang /_tog gi 'od dang /_dge ba dang /_tshangs pa dang /_skyes mchog dang /_spyan
[\[16b\]]
[\[16b.1\]]sdug pa dang /_klus byin pa dang /_bden pa'i tog dang /_brgyan pa dang /_zhum pa med pa'i dbyangs dang /_rin chen 'od dang /_dbyangs byin dang /_seng ge dang /_'od zer sna tshogs dang /_ye shes dpa' bo dang /_pad+ma'i phung po dang /_me tog rgyas pa dang /_mthu rtsal stobs dang /_
[\[16b.2\]]bsod nams phung po dang /_gzugs mchog dang /_skar mkhan dang /_zla ba'i sgron ma dang /_gzi brjid phung po dang /_byang chub rgyal po dang /_mi zad pa dang /_mngon rtogs spyan dang /_yan lag rgyas pa dang /_yul 'khor dang /_shes rab dang /_mchog dang /_gzi brjid
[\[16b.3\]]tshim mdzad dang /_shes rab 'byin dang /_'jam pa'i dbyangs dang /_chags pa med pa'i mdzod dang /_gtso bos byin dang /_gtso bo dang /_ye shes mthu rtsal dang /_'od 'phro can dang /_dbang po dang /_shugs 'chang dang /_skar rgyal dang /_'od bzangs dang /_grags pa byin
[\[16b.4\]]dang /_gzugs bzang po dang /_rgyal po dang /_don grub pa dang /_seng ge'i sde dang /_nor bu'i lha dang /_grags pa dang /_rgyal ba dang /_rgyal chen snying po dang /_bsod nams 'od zer dang /_smrang 'don pa dang /_sgron ma'i rgyal po dang /_ye shes brtsegs pa dang /_lha mchog
[\[16b.5\]]dang /_sa bdag dang /_rnam grol brnyes dang /_gtsug gi gser dang /_sgra gcan bzang bo dang /_thub dka' dang /_thub gsal dang /_zla ba'i 'od zer dang /_gser gyi 'od dang /_legs byin dang /_lha'i yon yan dbang po dang /_chos kyi gdugs dang /_bsod nams lag
[\[16b.6\]]dang /_chags med dang /_ye shes gya nom dang /_blo zhib mo dang /_gzi byin thams cad dang /_rtsi sman dang /_rnam grol tog dang /_'od kyi mdzod dang /_ye shes rgyal po dang /_'jigs mdzad dang /_chu bo sbong ba dang /_thogs med grags pa dang /_bden pa'i phung po dang /_
[\[16b.7\]]dbyangs snyan dang /_ri dbang mtshungs dang /_chos brtsegs dang /_thar ba'i gzi byin dang /_legs 'dzin dang /_rab tu zhi ba'i sku dang /_yid du 'ong ba'i gsung dang /_blo sbyangs pa dang /_chu lha dang /_'gro bas mchod dang /_seng ge'i logs dang /_chos kyi mthu rtsal dang /_skal
[\[17a\]]
[\[17a.1\]]pa bzang po dang /_mi 'khrugs pa'i mdog dang /_gzi brjid rgyal bo dang /_rtogs mdzad dang /_spyan legs pa dang /_don la gnas pa'i blo mnga' ba dang /_snang ba'i 'od zer dang /_spos kyi gzi brjid dang /_kun du dga' bar mdzad pa dang /_/don yod par
[\[17a.2\]]gshegs pa dang /_khro ba bcom dang /_gzugs mchog dang /_legs gshegs dang /_rab tu sbyin par grags dang /_'od gtsang dang /_lha'i nyi ma dang /_shes rab byin pa dang /_mnyam par gzhag pa'i bdag nyid dang /_gzi mdangs dang /_rgyal rigs dang /_skal
[\[17a.3\]]ldan shing rta dang /_gser mchog dang /_rnam par grol ba'i gtsug lag dang /_chos ldan dang /_spos gnas dang /_dregs spangs dang /_ye shes mdzod dang /_tshangs par gshegs dang /_tsan+dan dang /_mya ngan med dang /_seng ge'i 'od zer dang /_yul 'khor tog dang /_pad+ma'i
[\[17a.4\]]snying bo dang /_gzi brjid mtha' yas dang /_lha'i 'od zer dang /_shes rab tog dang /_mkhas pa dang /_ye shes 'byor ldan dang /_tshangs pa'i dbyig dang /_phyag na rin chen dang /_dbang ldan dang /_rdzogs par gsungs dang /_mchog tu gsungs dang /_mchod 'os dang /_
[\[17a.5\]]skar rgyal dang /_nyi ma dang /_'dam las rgal ba dang /_ye shes brnyes pa dang /_grub pa dang /_rma bya dang /_chos byin dang /_phan par bzhed pa dang /_ye shes ldan pa dang /_grags pa dang /_'od zer dra ba dang /_rnam par bcom pa dang /_bai DUr+ya'i snying po dang /_me tog dang /_
[\[17a.6\]]lha'i rgyal po dang /_zla ba dang /_dran pa'i 'od dang /_dge ba'i 'od dang /_yon tan mchog ma kun gyi 'od dang /_rin po che'i dpal dang /_skyes bu zla ba dang /_sgra gcan dang /_bdud rtsi'i 'od dang /_'jig rten gyi mchog dang /_skar ma'i 'od dang /_zhi ba'i stobs dang /_ye shes rgya mtsho
[\[17a.7\]]dang /_ri bo'i dbang po dang /_rab tu zhi ba dang /_yon tan mtha' yas ba'i stobs dang /_lha'i dbang po dang /_dbyangs snyan dang /_ngos bzangs dang /_don la gnas pa dang /_yon tan gzi brjid dpal dang /_mkhyen ldan zla med dang /_nga ro dpag med dang /_'od bzangs dang /_
[\[17b\]]
[\[17b.1\]]shin tu thugs gzhungs dang /_don dgongs gti mug bral ba dang /_dbyangs kyi yan lag khyad 'phags dang /_mchog tu mdzes par gshegs dang /_zhi ba'i don dang /_skyon med dang /_blo sbyangs dge ba dang /_pad+ma'i mdzod dang /_'od zer bzang po dang /_spobs pa'i
[\[17b.2\]]mdog dang /_stegs bzang po dang /_tshogs kyi dbang po dang /_bsnyengs pa dang bral ba dang /_ye shes bzhed pa dang /_spobs pa'i spyan dang /_blo'i mchog dang /_zla ba dang /_rin chen zla 'od dang /_bsnyengs pa med pa dang /_gzigs pa med pa dang /_tshangs pa'i dbyangs dang /_
[\[17b.3\]]dbyangs bzang po dang /_shes rab chen po'i stegs dang /_blo gros zla med dang /_rdo rje mkhregs pa dang /_byang chub blo gros dang /_ljon shing dbang po dang /_gdangs snyan pa dang /_bsod nams kyi stobs dang /_mthu'i dpal rnams so/_/shar la sogs pa'i sgo bzhi ru/_/
[\[17b.4\]]rnal 'byor ma rnams rim bzhin du/_/dkar mo chom rkun ro langs ma/_/za phod ma yang rnam par dgod/_/grwa la gnas pa'i lha mo bzhi/_/sbos mo ri khrod ma de bzhin/_/gtum mo dang ni g.yung mo ste/_/rim pas sngon bzhin brtag ces bya/_/dkyil 'khor 'khor lo gsum
[\[17b.5\]]pa la/_/dga' ba bzhi ni dag pa yis/_/kun nas ri mo bzhi can no/_/phyi rol dur khrod 'khor lo ni/_/chu yi dkyil 'khor dbus su ste/_/byis pa gsod dang lhag ma za/_/g.yul drag po dang mche ba kun/_/shar la sogs pa g.yon skor du/_/de ltar brtse ba chen pos bsam/_/
[\[17b.6\]]ru ba mun nag nang gi me/_/hA hA'i sgra dang sgra chen no/_/shing ni tsan+dan ga pur dang /_/dzA ti pha la dang e la/_/nA ga ge sar tsam pa dang /_kun du ru dang lha yi shing /_/phyogs skyong rnam ni mtshon bya ba/_/nyi ma bsil ba sa yi bu/_/ri bong can skyes bla ma nyid/_/ngan spang nyi ma'i
[\[17b.7\]]bu de bzhin/_/lha min mgo bor shes bya ste/_/drag po'i gdong rnams su bya'o/_/'bar ba ral gri chu gri dang /_/mdung rings spu gri brag de bzhin/_/glog dang sna tshogs mtshon 'bebs bar/_/dur khrod kyi ni dbus su bya/_/ral gri mig sman ri lu dang /_/rkang pa byug dang bcud
[\[18a\]]
[\[18a.1\]]len dang /_mchil lham dngul chus 'og gi_/dngos grub bsgrub pa mkhas par bya/_/zhes bya ba ni ye shes kyi 'khor lo ste/_/longs spyod rdzogs pa'i dkyil 'khor 'khor lo gsum gyi bdag nyid do//_//de nas de yi phyi rol 'chad/_/thugs
[\[18a.2\]]kyi 'khor lo 'di gsal ba'o/_/mdog rnams sum cu rtsa drug rtsibs/_/thams cad rang bzhin skyes pa mchog_/klu mo gnod sbyin mo 'byung mo/_/yi dwags dmyal mo mnar med ma/_/lhung ba mo dang bar med ma/_/bum mo gshin rje ma de bzhin/_/thig nag ma dang me
[\[18a.3\]]mdag mo/_/tsha ba mo dang rab tsha mo/_/ngu 'bod ma dang ngu 'bod che/_/mar nag du 'tshed ri gnyis 'tshir/_/sdang ma rmongs ma phrag dog ma/_/chags myos ser sna skud pa ma/_/grang ma ral gri'i nags ma nyid/_/rngu ma dang ni mu ge ma/_/nang dgon ma dang mtshon gyi dang /_/chu yi
[\[18a.4\]]dgon pa ma dang ni/_/ral gri sen mo rab med ma/_/spu gri'i so ma 'khor lo ma/_/grul bum mo ste lha mo che/_/mdag ni 'khor lo ji 'dra ba'o/_/phyag na mtshon cha sngon bzhin du/_/shes bya rang gi gzugs can no/_/de la nye ba'i dur khrod dang /_/de nas sa na chos kyi sprin/_/
[\[18a.5\]]sems kyi rang bzhin dag pa nyid/_/kun 'gro 'khor lo can du 'dod/_/rang bzhin spangs pas bdag med pa/_/'khor lo can sar bzhugs pa'o/_/'khor lo rnams ni rim ji bzhin/_/thams cad de ltar shes par bya/_/gnas bzhi rnams la bcu gnyis so/_/de ltar
[\[18a.6\]]bcu drug ces bya ba/_/stong pa nyid du mkhas pa yi/_/ye shes rnam shes ngo bo'i phyir/_/dur khrod bcom ldan 'das rang nyid/_/sprul pa'i 'khor lo 'di la ni/_/gsum gyi bdag nyid ming gis so/_/phyi nas gzhan ni thams cad ni/_/'khor lo gnyis su shes
[\[18a.7\]]par bya/_/thugs kyi 'khor lo'i dang po'o//_//de nas phyi rol du gzhan pa/_/gsung gi 'khor lo de bshad pa/_/dmar po btsod kyi kha dog ste/_/sum cu drug rtsibs bdag nyid gtso/_/mchod pa za ma gnyis ma dang /_/le lo ma chos sems sgom mo/_/khyim sems bud
[\[18b\]]
[\[18b.1\]]med sems ma dang /_/don sems ma dang sbyong bral ma/_/bu sems rnams dang mya ngan nam/_/bsam gtan ma dang sngags zlos ma/_/ngo tsha nga rgyal gdungs pa mo/_/sems can don byed brtson ma dang /_/rgyal po sems ma gzhan gnod ma/_/ye shes thob ma dka' thub ma/_/
[\[18b.2\]]rgas ma 'chi ba'i bsam can ma/_/bde ma sdug ma mi dge ma/_/yod dang med dang gnyis dang ni/_/bla ma sems ma 'gre ba mo/_/bzod ma mi bzod ma ngal ma/_/ngal sos ma dang bkres pa mchog_/las ni thams cad byed lha mo/_/rang bzhin 'khor lo 'di che ba'o/_/
[\[18b.3\]]kha dog rang bzhin 'khor lor grags/_/lhag ma 'dir ni sngon bzhin no/_/shes rab thabs bdag nyid lha mo/_/rang bzhin gyis ni dkyil 'khor 'di/_/gdan bzhi pa'i rgyud stong phrag ni/_/bcu gnyis pa las bshad pa ste/_/ye shes mkha' 'gro ma sogs kyi/_/mchod sogs lha
[\[18b.4\]]mor 'dod pa bzhin/_/grong mtha'i gnas ni 'di lta bu/_/kun du 'od kyi sa yin no/_/de ltar ye shes sogs sku'i mtha'/_/rlung me chu dang nam mkha' yis/_/bskor ba'i 'khor lo zhes bya bas/_/rdo rje mchog mang shes par par bya/_/zhes bya ba ni gsung gi 'khor lo'i gnyis pa sprul ba'i
[\[18b.5\]]'khor lo'o//_//de nas sku yi 'khor lo bshad/_/sku gsung thugs kyi kha dog can/_/sum cu rtsa drug dbyibs 'dra ba/_/rnal 'byor ma 'khor sgyur ma'o/_/rgyal chen bzhi yi rigs ma dang /_/sum cu rtsa gsum 'khor sgyur ma/_/'thab bral dga' ldan 'khor sgyur ma/_/
[\[18b.6\]]'phrul dga' ma dang de bzhin du/_/gzhan 'phrul dbang byed ma dang ni/_/tshangs ris ma yi 'khor lo ma/_/tshangs pa mdun 'don ma de bzhin/_/tshangs pa chen po 'khor sgyur ma/_/'od chung tshad med 'od ma dang /_/'od gsal ma dang dge chung ma/_/tshad med dge ba'i 'khor
[\[18b.7\]]sgyur ma/_/dge rgyas ma dang sprin med ma/_/bsod nams skyes ba'i 'khor lo dang /_/'bras bu che ba'i 'khor sgyur ma/_/mi che mi gdung 'khor sgyur ma/_/shin tu mthong ma bzang snang ma/_/'og min ma yi 'khor sgyur ma/_/nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched ma/_/rnam shes mtha'
[\[19a\]]
[\[19a.1\]]yas skye mched ma/_/ci'ang med skye mched ma de nas/_/'du shes 'du shes med min ma/_/dmyal mo yi dgas ma de bzhin/_/dus 'gro mi mo lha min mo/_/gzhal med mkha' spyod ma de bzhin/_/zla mo nyi mo gshin rje mo/_/dbang mo 'khor sgyur mar shes bya/_/rang
[\[19a.2\]]gi 'khor lo'i mdog bzhin bya/_/phyag dang mtshon cha sngar bzhin no/_/shes rab thabs kyi rang bzhin te/_/nye ba'i grong mthar yang dag gnas/_/sa ni mos par spyod pa'o/_/de nas de yi phyi khyams la/_/'phags pa dgyes pa dang /_mthu stobs dang /_/skar mal dgyes pa dang /_
[\[19a.3\]]sprin gyi rnga sgra dang /_/spyan sdug zhal dang /_/ye shes bzang ldan dang /_'byor ldan dang /_yon tan phung po dang /_gsal ba dang /_chos kyi rgyal mtshan dang /_ye shes nga ro dang /_nam mkha' dang /_mchod sbyin nga ro dang /_shes rab rnam dgod nga ro dang /_yon tan 'od zer gzi
[\[19a.4\]]brjid dang /_drang srong dbang po dang /_blo ldan dang /_stobs pa'i tshogs dang /_mchod sbyin bzang po dang /_zla ba'i zhal dang /_shin tu gzigs dang /_rdul bral dang /_yon tan tshogs dang /_tog ldan dang /_bsod nams rgyal mtshan dang /_yul 'khor spobs pa dang /_
[\[19a.5\]]rin chen rab sbyin dang /_zla dgyes dang /_seng ge'i stobs dang /_dbang sgyur rgyal po dang /_bdud rtsi gsal ba dang /_bsam gtan snyoms dang /_'khrul ba med pa dang /_dri ma rab tu zhi ba dang /_phyogs ma bslad dang /_mdzes pa dang /_/zhal bzangs dang /_shugs gnas ye
[\[19a.6\]]shes ldan dang /_gsung gi dbang po dang /_gzi brjid chen po dang /_blo gros zab mo dang /_bdud rtsi dang /_chos kyi stobs dang /_/me tog 'od dang /_khams gsum dag gi mchod pa'i gnas dang /_sgra gcan nyi mar snying bo dang /_lha'i mchod pa dang /_

[\[37a.1\]]hUM oM pa ra spa ra a nu pra biSh+TiH sarba d+harmA hUM/_oM a t+yan tA nu pra piSh+TaHsarba d+harmA hUM zhes brjod pas/_lag pa rdo rje rtse lnga bar bsgoms te thal mo kha phye la lag par gtor ma bzhag la rnam pa gsum dbyer med pa'i ngo bor lhag par dmigs te/_lha mo tshad ma'o dam
[\[37a.2\]]tshig tshad ma de/_/des gsungs dag kyang mchog tu tshad ma'o/_/des ni bden bar gyur cig 'di ru ni/_/lha mos bdag la rjes 'dzin rgyur gyur cig_/ces brjod de lha rnams kyis ljags hUM dkar po las rdo rje bsams la oM a ral+li hoHdzaHhUM baM hoH/_/badzra DA ki ni sa ma ya s+t+waM dr-i sh+ya hoH/_/

[\[37a.4\]]pa'i don la bslang ba dang /_bkra shis brjod pa dang /_yi ge brgya ba brjod par bya'o/_/de nas dur khrod pa rnams kyi lce byin gyis brlabs te oM kha kha khA hi khA hi sarba yak+Sha rAk+Sha sa/_b+hU ta pre ta pi shA tsa un+mA da/_a pa smA ra DA ka DA ki n+ya da ya i maM ba liM gr-ih+Na n+tu sarba sid+d+hi m+me pra ya ts+tsha n+tu ya
[\[37a.5\]]thai baM ya thaiSh+TaM/_b+hu ny+dza tha/_pi wa tha mA ti kra ma tha ma ma sarba karta ya/_sah+phu kha bi brid+d+ha ye ma ma sa hA yi ka b+ha wa n+tu hUM hUM phaT swA hA/_zhes bya ba lan gsum brjod pas thams cad kyis 'thungs par bsam mo/_/de nas de rnams la yang mchod pa la sogs pa thams cad
[\[37a.6\]]sngar bzhin byas la/_srid dang zhi ba mnyam pas zhen pa bcom zhing kun du rtog pa bcom/_/dngos dang dngos po ma yin thams cad mkha' bzhin rnam par gzigs pa rnams/_/bla ma mchog gi thugs rje'i chu spro thugs ni chu yi mgon po rnams/_/mdzod cig mdzod cig lha mos bdag
[\[37a.7\]]la rjes su thugs ni brtse bar mdzod/_/ces brjod la mig gi phyag rgya bstan la pad+ma'i lag pas bskor/_lte bar 'khyud pas se gol gtogs te/_oM badzra maN+Dal muHzhes brjod pas dkyil 'khor bdag nyid mdzod spu nas gzhug par bya ste/_rol mo dang mar me'i snang ba dang bcas pas bskyal
[\[37b\]]
[\[37b.1\]]par bya'o/_/gtor ma'i cho ga bya ba las/_/byung ba'i dge bas 'gro ba kun/_/lus sems bde bas gnas gyur cig_/stobs bcu dang yang ldan par shog_/dpal mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i rgyud kyi gtor ma'i cho ga rin po che asma gan+b+ha mkhas pa dza ya se na'i gsung dpal ye shes rdo

[\[37b.3\]]thog mar bla ma'i mdun du'am gzhan du yang rung ste chu dang me tog la sogs pa tshogs par byas la rkang pa bkrus te/_oM hrIHswA hA/_zhes bya bas lag par bkru ba dang /_kha bshal bar bya'o/_/oM hUM zhes bya bas bdag dang gnas dang rnal 'byor bsrung bar bya'o/_/de nyid kyis
[\[37b.4\]]stan byin gyis brlab pa yang bya'o/_/oM badzra b+hu mi hUM zhes bya bas sa gzung bar bya'o/_/oM sarba big+h+nan uta sa ra ya hUM swA hA/_zhes bya bas chu dang lci ba srog chags med pas byug par bya'o/_/oM AHbadzra re khe hUM zhes bya bas lag pa g.yas pas me tog g.yon pa'i rgyab tu bzhag
[\[37b.5\]]la maN+Dal du dor ro/_/oM su re khe sarba ta thA ga ta a d+hi tiSh+Tha n+tu swA hA/_zhes bya bas lag pa bkru bar bya'o/_/oM ma Ni d+ha ri badzra Ni ma hA pra ti sA ri rak+Sha rak+Sha maM hUM hUM phaT phaT swA hA/_zhes bya bas rang gi mgo bo la me tog bzhag pas bdag nyid bsrung bar bya'o/_/de nas maN+Dal de nyin mo

[\[38a\]]
[\[38a.1\]]skad cig gi sbyor bas dbus kyi me tog gi steng du rdo rje sems dpa'i rol pas bzhugs pa'i bla ma bsgom par bya'o/_/de nas phyogs bzhir rim pa bzhin du sngo ba dang ljang ba dang dmar ba dang /_ser ba'i kha dog can/_thams cad mdzes ma/_dga' ba'i mchog

[\[38a.3\]]tshogs pa'i mchod pa'i snyim pas gtso bo la stobs par byed pa dang /_me la sogs pa'i mtshams rnams su dkar ba dang sngo ba dang dmar ba dang ljang ba'i kha dog can gyi/_sangs rgyas spyan ma dang /_mA ma kI dang /_gos dkar mo dang /_sgrol ma rnams zhal gcig phyag gnyis ma/_

[\[38a.7\]]gsung /_dpal ye shes rdo rjes bsgyur ba rdzogs so//[ {D1520}]@##/_/rgya gar skad du/_shrI tsakra sam+ba ra sto t+t+ra nA ma/_bod skad du/_dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i bstod pa zhes bya ba/_bcom ldan 'das he ru ka la phyag 'tshal lo/_/hUM/_chos nyid dbyings las

[\[38b.1\]]bzhengs pa'i sku mchog ni/_/nyon mongs rnam dag ye shes sku brnyes shing /_/dus mtha'i me dpung lta bu'i klong dkyil nas/_/ri rab chu skyes nyi ma'i gdan steng na/_/zhal gcig phyag gnyis dpa' bo chen po'i sku/_/zhabs gnyis brkyang bskum 'jigs byed dus mtshan mnan/_/

[\[39a.1\]]kyis bdag bstod na/_/mkha' dang mnyam pa'i 'gro ba ma lus kun/_/mgon po khyod kyis thugs rjes gzung du gsol/_/dam tshig brtul zhugs spyod pa'i rnal 'byor la/_/brtse ba'i thugs kyis bu bzhin dgongs nas kyang /_/bar chad bdud dpung zhi bar mdzad du gsol/_/dur

[\[40a.1\]]'gyur/_/zhes sems skyed de/slob ma la 'di skad brjod par bya'o/_/'khor ba'i rgya mtshor bying ba ni/_/de rnams nyon mongs 'dam gyis gos/_/rgal bar mi nus pa yi sems/_/shin tu sdug bsngal tshogs rnams la/_/nyan thos la sogs

[\[40b\]]
[\[40b.1\]]gi lha yi rnal 'byor ni/_/mngon par rtogs pa bshad pa yi/_/rim pa legs par bsgom ldan pas/_/bdag po'i rim pa 'bum phrag gcig_/yum gyi de phyed 'khor gyi khri/_/gsang sngags rgyal po ma nyams bzla/_/de dag ni sngon du bsnyen pa'i cho ga'o/_/dkyil 'khor

[\[41a\]]
[\[41a.1\]]na rlung chen 'byung /_/rus par bcas la zug rngu 'byung /_/gseg mar bcas na lkugs par 'gyur/_/phub ma sol ba la ni rims/_/skra dang rtsa ba shing sogs bcas/_/gnod pa phra mo 'byung bar 'gyur/_/de phyir shis pa 'dod pa yis/_/'bad pas sa yi
[\[41a.2\]]cha sbyang bya/_/dkyil 'khor khru ni brgyad par 'dod/_/gzhan dag rgyal po la khru brgyad/_/mtha' skyes rnams kyi de yi phyed/_/gtso bo rnams kyi de'i phyed gsungs/_/tshong dpon rnams kyi khru bcu gnyis/_/sgrub po rnams kyi khru drug pa/_/dkyil 'khor rim pa 'di gsungs pa/_/

[\[64a.3\]]rin chen 'byung ldan rnal 'byor gyis/_/tshig ni rtsub mo la sogs pas/_/bla med dngos grub thob par 'gyur/_/'od dpag med kyi brdzun ngag smra/_/don yod grub mchog ting 'dzin gyis/_/blo ldan rgyud gsungs cho ga yis/_/dam tshig dag pa bsten par bya/_/zhes

[\[64a.5\]]rdo rje'i 'khor lo bskor bar gyis/_/de bzhin gshegs kun rgyal ba rgyal/_/bdag po'i 'khor lo bskor bar gyis/_/zhes so/_/rjes su gnang ba'i dbang bskur ba'i cho ga'o//_//de ltar byas nas de nas phyis/_/rtsa ba'i dkyil 'khor du zhugs nas/_/dkyil
[\[64a.6\]]'khor bltas nas gsang sngags kyi/_/bskul bar smra ba sbyin par bya/_/ting 'dzin sngags kyi rgyal po yis/_/byin nas gsang ba brtsam par bya/_/rgyud 'dir gsungs pa'i dam pa'i rdzas/_/mkhas pa yis ni bza' bar bya/_/de nas steng du langs pa yis/_/sangs
[\[64a.7\]]rgyas kun bdag rnal 'byor brtson/_/rdo rje'i ming dbang bskur ba yis/_/'di skad de bzhin gshegs lung bstan/_/de la 'di'i rim brjod bya ste/_/mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho dpal gzugs kyis/_/slob ma de bzhin yongs bzhag nas/_/rang yang bdag po'i sbyor ba ldan/_/chos
[\[64b\]]
[\[64b.1\]]gos lag pa g.yon pa yis/_/'dzin pa'i tshul gyis de bzhin du/_/mngon par mchog sbyin tshul nyid kyis/_/mnyam par gzhag pas 'di skad brjod/_/ngas 'di khyod la lung bstan bya/_/rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs/_/srid pa shin du dag pa'i phyir/_/srid pa'i
[\[64b.2\]]ngan 'gro las bton nas/_/kye dpal che ge mo rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa grub pa khyod kyi dam tshig go zhes bya ba'o/_/gang gis cho ga 'di yis ni/_/phyag rgya chen po'i tshul gang gis/_/gang la lung bstan byed bzhin pa/_/dpal he ru ka sogs lha dang /_/sangs
[\[64b.3\]]rgyas byang chub sems rnams dang /_/dkyil 'khor du gnas rnams dang /_/dam tshig gcod pa'i mgrin pa yis/_/rdzogs pa'i byang chub bstan pa mdzad/_/'di ltar 'di'i phyag rgya chen pos mchog tu gsang ba chen po bzang po bden pa'i byin gyi rlabs
[\[64b.4\]]kyis 'grub par 'gyur te 'di'i tshig gis zhes bya ba la dad par bya'o zhes bya ba nyid brjod nas phyis/_/yang dag dbugs dbyung sbyin par bya/_/gsang mchog dkyil 'khor dam par ni/_/bltas nas su ni rab zhugs pas/_/sdig pa kun las rnam nges grol/_/de ring
[\[64b.5\]]legs par gnas par 'gyur/_/bde chen theg pa 'di la ni/_/slar yang 'chi ba yod pa min/_/mi tshugs pa dang mi choms par/_/'jigs pa med pas rol par gyis/_/srid pa'i sdug bsngal las ni 'das/_/srid pa shin tu dag pa'i phyir/_/dngos grub dam pa
[\[64b.6\]]sdom pa ni/_/'di ni rtag tu bsrung bar gyis/_/rjes gnang mchog tu dbugs 'byin pa/_/sangs rgyas kun dngos rab tu gsungs/_/rdo rje zhes gang phyag rgya dang /_/byang chub sems ni mi spang zhing /_/gang zhig bskyed pa tsam gyis ni/_/sangs rgyas nyid du dogs med

[\[65a\]]
[\[65a.1\]]sangs rgyas/_/rdo rje dril bu phyag rgya yang /_/nam yang spang bar mi bya'o/_/slob dpon smad par mi bya'o/_/'di ni sangs rgyas kun dang mnyam/_/gang zhig slob dpon la smod la/_/bla ma sangs rgyas kun dang mnyam/_/sangs rgyas thams cad smad pas
[\[65a.2\]]na/_/de ni rtag tu sdug bsngal 'thob/_/rims dang dug dang dbyig dug nad/_/mkha' 'gros 'tshe dang gdon rnams dang /_/bgegs dang log 'dren drag rnams kyis/_/bsad nas dmyal bar ltung bar byed/_/de phyir kun nas rab 'bad pas/_/rdo rje slob dpon
[\[65a.3\]]bla ma che/_/dge mchog rab tu mi spyoms pa/_/nam yang smad par mi bya'o/_/bla ma la gus de la yon/_/de nas rjes mthun dbul bar bya/_/de yis rims sogs gdung ba rnams/_/phyir zhing dbyung bar mi 'gyur ro/_/rtag tu rang gi dam tshig spyod/_/sbyin min bu dang
[\[65a.4\]]bu mo sogs/_/srog rnams kyis kyang bsten bya na/_/longs spyod g.yo ba smos ci dgos/_/gang phyir bskal pa bye rnams kyis/_/rtag tu rnyed par dka' ba yi/_/sangs rgyas nyid kyang brtson ldan pa/_/tshe 'di nyid la ster bar byed/_/rtag tu rang gi dam tshig bsgrub/_/
[\[65a.5\]]rtag tu de bzhin gshegs pa mchod/_/rtag tu bla ma la yang dbul/_/'di ni sangs rgyas kun dang mnyam/_/de byin sangs rgyas thams cad la/_/rtag tu byin pa nyid du 'gyur/_/de yis bsod nams tshogs yin te/_/tshogs las dngos grub mchog tu 'gyur/_/de
[\[65a.6\]]ring bdag skyes 'bras bur bcas/_/gang 'dir legs par rab tu gnas/_/dam tshig lha rnams dang mnyam mo/_/rang byung du ni da lta skyes/_/ding 'dir dbang bskur tshe ldan pa/_/rdo rje bcas sangs rgyas kun gyis/_/khams gsum gyi rgyal srid che yi/_/rgyal po
[\[65a.7\]]bdag pos gnas pa yin/_/di ring bdud las rgyal byas nas/_/grong khyer mchog tu rab tu zhugs/_/di ring sangs rgyas nyid thob par/_/khyod 'gyur bar ni the tshom med/_/zhes bya ba yi bka' drin rdo rje yid kyis te/_/rang gi dam tshig mi zad bde skyes bsten par gyis/_/
[\[65b\]]
[\[65b.1\]]shin tu skyes sla'i bde ba sangs rgyas kun gzugs brnyan/_/rtag pa nyid ni rtogs par 'gyur bar shog_/ces bya'o/_/bla ma yi ni zhabs gnyis la/_/gus pas mnyes gshin pas btud de/_/ji ltar gsungs shing bstan pa kun/_/ji lta'i dag rjes gnang zhes gsol/_/de

[\[65b.3\]]brtan/_/oM sarba ta thA ga sid+d+hi badzra sa ma ya tiSh+Tha e Sha twAM d+ha ra yA mi badzra satwa hi hi hi hi hUM/_zhes bya'o/_/'di skad gsang sngags brjod nas ni/_/'di skad bzhin du dril bu sbyin/_/'di de sangs rgyas thams cad kyi/_/shes rab dbyangs kyi rjes 'gror bshad/_/khyod kyis kyang ni
[\[65b.4\]]rtag tu bcang /_/byang chub mchog tu rgyal bas bzhed/_/ces so/_/de nas me tog dri la sogs/_/sgeg mo sogs pas mchod par bya/_/'dod pa'i yon tan lnga yis kyang /_/de bzhin gshegs rnams mchod byas nas/_/ci ltar bde bas slob ma rnams/_/shes rab sgo nas
[\[65b.5\]]mchod pa yang /_/spos sogs ji ltar 'dod pa yis/_/ji lta ba yi mchod par bya/_/ji lta ba 'byor bar gyur pa yis/_/zhugs pa'i slob ma bza' dang bcas/_/rnam pa sna tshogs ro'i bza' ba/_/myos byed btung ba sna tshogs dang /_/gang zhig rgyud gzhan la grags pa'i/_/glu
[\[65b.6\]]sgra nye bar spyod rnams kyis/_/'di don cho gas phul ba yi/_/bla ma'i bde bas yang dag mchod/_/de bzhin du ni yang gsungs pa/_/chang bcas chang min btung ba dang /_/ji ltar 'dod pa bsten par 'gyur/_/ji ltar 'dod pa'i longs spyod kyis/_/ji lta'i rim pas bsgom par bya/_/

[\[66a.1\]]nas phyi rol mchod sogs dang /_/yid 'byung rnams kyis gtso bo la/_/sngags pas gus pas mchod byas te/_/nyi ma shar ba'i dus su yang /_/dpal he ru ka ye shes che/_/zhes bya'i bstod pas ji ltar yang /_/legs par bstod nas de nas phyis/_/

[\[66b.1\]]nas dkyil 'khor sa gzhi la'o/_/mnga' bdag sku mdog sngon po rgyal gyur cig_/dmar pos ji ltar mdzes byas rgyal gyur cig_/dam tshig gis brgyan mdzes pa rgyal gyur cig_/zla phyed dbu la brgyan pa rgyal gyur cig_/lha mo'i 'khor los brgyan pa rgyal gyur cig_/dang

[\[67a\]]
[\[67a.1\]]par gyur rnams kyis/_/dpal he ru ka shes rab che/_/mkha' 'gro ma yi dra ba sdom/_/zhes bya'i rjes su gnang sems kyis/_/skor ba lan gsum byas nas ni/_/lus thams cad ni phab byas nas/_/ji ltar sngon bzhin phyag byas te/_/bdag nyid bla ma

[\[67a.5\]]pa dbyung ba de bzhin no/_/bde ba yis ni khrus byas te/_/bdag med sgom pa spyad par bya/_/slob dpon gyis ni de nas phyis/_/legs par bsdus pa'i yo byad nor/_/rang nyid kyis ni longs spyad de/_/slob ma rnams la mi bgo'o/_/dkyil 'khor gyis ni thabs thams cad/_/slob
[\[67a.6\]]dpon nyid la sbyar bar bya/_/gal te dam tshig can gyis ni/_/slob ma la ni nye bar sbyar/_/de ltar bdag gis legs par sbyar ba 'di rnams kyang rang gi rtog pa sna tshogs 'brel med cing lung dang mi ldan par bsdebs pa ni ma yin te/_dpal rdo rje phag mo'i le'u gnyis pa
[\[67a.7\]]las/_gang gis slob ma dbang bskur ba/_/de nyid bzhi rnams bcas pas so/_/theg pa chen por yongs smin la/_/phyi nas sngags ni rab bstan bya/_/sngon du phag mo'i dkyil 'khor ni/_/bri bya de nas he ru ka'i'o/_/rdo rje'i bu mo'am de nas gzhan/_/der ni shes rab
[\[67b\]]
[\[67b.1\]]gzhug par bya/_/rgyud gzhan du ni dbang bskur la/_/tshul 'di bstan par mi bya'o/_/zhes gsungs so/_/'on kyang rdo rje phag mo'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho gar ma sbyar te/_'di gzhan pas che ba nyid kyi phyir dang /_'di nyid kyis thams cad la sbyar bar bya ba'i phyir ro/_/chen

[\[67b.7\]]pa chen po dza ya se na'i gsung rin po che dbang gi rgyal po'i mdzod dpal ye shes rdo rje bsgyur ba rdzogs so//[ {D1522}]@/_/dpal mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga bzhugs/_/@##/_/bcom ldan 'das dpal mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho la phyag 'tshal lo/_/yod
[\[68a\]]
[\[68a.1\]]med mtha' sogs rnam par spangs/_/blo yi spyod yul ma yin kyang /_/'gro la brtse bas sna tshogs gzugs/_/mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho la phyag 'tshal/_/gang zhig blo yi mun sel cing /_/bde ba ma lus 'byung ba'i gnas/_/rdo rje sems dpa'i ngo bo nyid/_

[\[68a.5\]]kyi steng du sor bzhi dor bar dpangs dang rgyar sor bzhi pa'i kha khyer cung zad gyed pa bya'o/_/kha khyer gyi steng du dbus kyi mtshan mas bskor bar bya zhing /_phyi rol ni thams cad la gru bzhir byas te/_grwa bzhir yang de nyid kyis mtshan pa'o/_/kha khyer gyi 'og gi gyed pa la pad+ma

[\[68a.7\]]rgyas pa la ni sa gzhi ser po'i steng du thad kar khru do pa thur du khru gang ba la gru bzhi pa'o/_/de'i dbus su rin po che sor brgyad pa la rdo rjes mtshan pa'o/_/kha khyer thams cad ni bzhi cha'i rim pas dang /_de la dbus kyi mtshan mas bskor ba dang pad+ma 'dab ma bcu drug bri ba
[\[68b\]]
[\[68b.1\]]thun mong du go bar bya'o/_/de'i phyi rol khru phyed 'khor bar ba'i lci bas nye bar byugs la de gnyis sa ser po dang ldan pa dang /_dri ser pos byugs te me tog ser po dgram par bya'o/_/dbang gi thab ni sa gzhi dmar ba'am/_zhan par gru gsum pa khru phyed pa'o/_/dbus su pad+ma la
[\[68b.2\]]gnas pa'i pad+ma la rdo rjes mtshan pa'o/_/sa dmar po dang bdud rtsi dang bcas pa'i dris nye bar byugs la me tog dmar po gtor bar bya'o/_/phyi rol lci bas byug pa yang kun la shes par bya'o/_/mngon spyod ni gas pa dang /_ba tsha can dang /_rtsub pa dang /_nam mkha' ltar
[\[68b.3\]]gnag pa'i sa gzhi la zur drug pa sor brgyad pa'o/_/dbus su pad+ma la rdo rjes mtshan pa'o/_/yang na zhib la khru gnyis pa'o/_/rgyas pa la khru gsum pa'o/_/dbang la khru bzhi pa'o/_/mngon spyod la khru lnga pa'o/_/de'i kha khyer la sogs dang dbus kyi pad+ma'i mtshan ma la

[\[82a.2\]]mnyam nyid gnas pa'i sems kyis ni/_/rnal 'byor dbang phyug ldang ba na/_/mkha' 'gro ma yi bde ba'i mchog_/klus bskul ba ni dran par bya/_/thog mar bla ma mchod pa dang /_/rdo rje sems dpa'i rang bzhin las/_/dbang bskur rol ba'i bde chen po/_/skad cig gis ni kun
[\[82a.3\]]khyab pa'o/_/sku gsung thugs la gnas par bya/_/mnyam par ma bzhag rnal 'byor gyis/_/snying rje chen po'i yid kyis ni/_/khams gsum pa yi sems can kun/_/shrI he ru kar blta bya zhing /_/byang sems chu rgyun khrus bya ste/_/bcu phyed bdud rtsi'i zas las bza'/_/
[\[82a.4\]]gcer bu skra grol lhor bltas la/_/brtul zhugs can gyis gtor ma sbyin/_/gsang ba'i rim par bstan pa'o/_/spros pa kun la dmigs nas ni/_/spros pas spros pa med par bya/_/spros pa nyid ni spros med byed/_/spros bral bde ba chen po ste/_/brtan dang g.yo ba'i
[\[82a.5\]]'jig rten kun/_/ma lus lus pa med 'grub cing /_/de nyid myur ba nyid du yang /_/bde mchog dam pa 'grub pa yin/_/bcom ldan sku gsung thugs la bzhugs/_/A li kA li mnyam gnas pa/_/'khor lo la ni nges par bskor/_/steng du 'bar ba'i tshul gyis ni/_/
[\[82a.6\]]'og tu 'bab pa nges pa'i phyir/_/zag med dri med bde ba'i dngos/_/'chi med thig le'i ngo bo ni/_/sa bon tshul gyis 'bab par 'gyur/_/rtag tu snying gi dbus gnas pa/_/'od gsal bde ba chen po ni/_/nyi ma zla ba rnam dag pa/_/'char dang nub par bstan pa yin/_/

[\[82b.1\]]thabs dang shes rab snyoms 'jug cing /_/gnyis thim bcu drug cha phyed can/_/zag bcas bde med gnyis spangs pa/_/gsang ba dga' ba'i rang bzhin no/_/dam tshig gsang ba chen po yi/_/sku gsung thugs la mnyam med la/_/rang gi mtshan nyid ngo bo stong /_/rtog pa

[\[82b.3\]]na/_/mchog gi sku ni nges par 'thob/_/bsgom pa 'di ni mchog yin te/_/'dod pa'i dngos grub bla na med/_/rnal 'byor skye ba 'di nyid la/_/rdo rje 'chang gi sa thob pa'o/_/rnal 'byor ba rnams 'pho ba'i tshe/_/dpal ldan khrag 'thung la sogs pa/_/rnal 'byor ma
[\[82b.4\]]yi tshogs rnams kyis/_/me tog sna tshogs lag na thogs/_/rgyal mtshan ba dan sna tshogs dang /_/glu yi mchod pa sna tshogs kyis/_/'chi ba zhes 'di rnam rtog ste/_/mkha' spyod gnas su 'khrid par byed/_/dpal 'khor lo bde mchog gsang ba rin po che yid bzhin

[\[83a.1\]]mi snang bar gyur to/_/de'i ngang las bdag nyid kyi spyi bor a las bskyed pa'i steng du haM yig nag po las 'od zer 'phros pa las rdo rje/_de las bde mchog yab yum gnyis su med par 'khril ba'i lha'i sku 'ja' tshon nam/_chu zla shar ba lta bu'i sgyu ma'i

[\[84b.1\]]'byor gnyis su 'gyur/_/bde ba chen por rab tu bshad/_/sbyor ba'i lus ni thams cad las/_/rgyal ba rnams kyis spras par bshad/_/shin tu sbyangs la rab gnas pa'i/_/snod ldan bdag nyid chen pos bzung /_/lus sems bde bar spyad nas ni/_/nyin mtshan sbyor ba bsten

[\[85a.1\]]bran dang lam chen btsun mo'o/_/skal ldan rnams kyis rtogs par gyis/_/sa ma ya/_dam pa bde chen mgon po skye med rang byung sangs rgyas yin/_/e ma ho/_/smin grol sems kyi rgya mdud shig_/phyi nang gsang ba mthar thug pas/_/dbang gis rnam par rtog

[\[86a\]]
[\[86a.1\]]nyi ma gsum sgom pa'i brda chu bo med dang rin chen gsum lta ba'i brda'o/_/rdo rje mkha' 'gro mas ro snyoms rnam pa gsum bstan pa/_sha za smyon pa ce spyang gsum lud kyi ro snyoms ro langs sar sa bu chung gsum brtul zhugs kyi ro snyoms nam mkha' sprin dang

[\[86a.3\]]brda'o/_/'bras bu mthar phyin pa la rang bzhin cos nyid klong du gnas pa/_snang ba dag par 'char ba/_'od gsal du song ba/_sku gsum lhun gyis grub pa/_ngo bo spros pa dang bral ba/_skye med tin pas btsal du med pa'o/_/rdo rje tshig rkang yin no rdzogs so//_//
[\[86a.4\]{D1529}]@##/_/rgya gar skad du/_shrI sam+ba ra u pa de sha mu kha kar+N+Na pa ra tsin+ta ma Ni nA ma/_bod skad du/_dpal sdom pa'i man ngag zhal nas snyan du brgyud pa yid bzhin nor bu zhes bya ba/_dpal rdo rje sems dpa' la phyag 'tshal lo/_/sku gsum bdag nyid dgos 'byung bla ma
[\[86a.5\]]dam pa'i zhabs pad ze 'bru dri med 'od zer la phyag 'tshal/_/gsang sngags mthar thug snying po'i bcud byung yid bzhin nor bu mkha' 'gro'i gsung bzhin rtogs pas 'dir gsal bkod/_/bde gshegs thugs la snang ba dri med pany+tsa pa nas rtogs pa ki ri li ru gsang bdag mnyes/_/
[\[86a.6\]]spyod pas zil mnan lus kyi bkod pas rnal 'byor rjes bzung mdzad pa mtha' yas 'gro rnams stong par byas/_/bslab pa gsum dang rgyud par ldan pa nyams su myong bas 'jug tshul shes pas bla ma dam par shes/_/paN+Di pa dang rigs chad bral ltar rus sbal spu ste mo gsham bu ltar
[\[86a.7\]]slob ma skyon lnga bral/_/mchog gi don 'dod gang gis de bstan thog mar dbang bzhis rgyud smin thabs dang shes rab 'brel ba nyid/_/'di don rim par brgyud pa rna bar 'pho byed de tshe sangs rgyas bstan gnas gus par mnyan par gyis/_/sa yi cho ga lhag par gnas pa rig byed slob dpon
[\[86b\]]
[\[86b.1\]]rig sbyor sogs kyis bum pa'i dbang bskur bya/_/bslab pas rgyud mdzes thos bsam nor ldan bla mar 'os pa phul la bla mas gsal stong la sogs bskur/_/nyer lnga lhag spangs rigs ldan rgyan spras zag bcas bskul sogs gsum pa byin nas brtul zhugs brtan par bya/_/
[\[86b.2\]]dga' ba gsum son lhan cig skyes pa rnyog pa dang bral yul du byas sogs 'bras bur shes par gyis/_/dbang bzhi dang 'brel brda yis mtshon pa shes rab bdag nyid sin+d+hu ra la mnyes sogs ston mos brgyan/_/slob dpon bzhi la dbang bzhi dus bzhi byed pa bcu gnyis chos nyid
[\[86b.3\]]dbang la mtshon du med par byos/_/dbang gis smin nas rim pa gnyis shes rnal 'byor dbang phyug zung 'jug rgyal ba'i sku bsgrub phyir/_/dbang po'i rim pas dbye dang bsdu ba'i rim pa shes nas 'du 'dzi med pas rgyun du 'bad pas spyad/_/tshangs pa'i gnas bzhi gsol dang khams
[\[86b.4\]]sogs bslab pa 'khor lo tshogs brten rgyu 'bras nyid dang phra mor brjod/_/go cha ye shes rgyas gdab sku gsung mchod dang bzlas pa rdzogs rim phrin las phyogs dang thub pa nyid/_/bsdus pa'i sbyor ba tshad med bzhi ldan rdzus te skyes pa skad cig rnal 'byor bzlas pas bcas pa nyid/_/
[\[86b.5\]]brtan g.yo'i dngos po lhan cig skyes pa snang sems dbyer med non po'i spyod yul zung 'jug rdo rje'i sku/_/kun la khyab pa ngo bo nyid ston gsal rig mtshan nyid thub pa'i dbang po bde gshegs kun gyi gtso/_/gsum gsal bdag gis mngon sum nyid du legs par rtogs nas sgom
[\[86b.6\]]dang bzlas pa gsal por rab tu phye/_/chos dbyings skye med rgyal ba'i yum gcig rgyan dang phyogs dang rgyal ba nyid de nam mkha'i ri mor blta/_/brtan dang g.yo ba rten dang brten pa lha yi rang bzhin rang la bcug nas sna yi rtse mor rdo rje bzlas/_/gtor ma byin nas dbang po 'bring pos
[\[86b.7\]]'od gsal bsgoms te dbang sogs lam dang dam tshig 'bras bur bsre/_/bdag 'jug dbang dang bla ma mchod byed nyams chags bskang phyir rdo rje sems dpa' brtan pa'i cho ga bzlas/_/rgyal po blon po dmangs kyi byed pas mtshams kyi kun spyod za nyal 'gro dang khrus sogs rnal

[\[87a.1\]]'byor bya/_/rnam rtog dang bral zla ba drug tu nges par bsams na grub pa'i mtshan ma mthong nas rol par gnas/_/thub pa'i bstan pa rgyas mdzad dngos grub mthar 'byin zab dang rgya che gnyis med dam tshig kun gyi gzhi/_/bag yod bsgom zhing brten dang
[\[87a.2\]]gsang ba mi gsal mi 'bral bza' bsrung mchog gyur thub pas rab tu gsungs/_/bslab pa gsum dang rgyu 'bras zhen med dbang sogs 'bras bu rgyud gzhan las gsungs rang sems dran pas bsrung /_/sku gsum la brten ting 'dzin gsum gyis rgya cher rab gsal gzhi lam
[\[87a.3\]]'bras bus lta ba mtshon par gyis/_/rnal 'byor srog rtsol sangs rgyas lnga bdag g.yon dang g.yas su rim pa ji bzhin rgyu ma nges pa ste/_/mnyam par gzhag pas 'jug pa'i rlung nyid bum pa can du byas nas brtan pa'i go 'phang so sor thob/_/rlung gi sbyor ba de nyid las dang mi
[\[87a.4\]]shes las dang las min 'grub rig pas ni 'bras bu ster/_/bsdams pa che dang bzlas pa'i rim pa goms pas dge dang mi dge 'chi bzlog rlung rig pas ni shes/_/dbye dang phyed las chos mtshungs rgyun mtshan bsdam pa'i sbyor ba'i bskyed rim goms pas mthun pa'i rkyen dang ldan/_/

[\[87a.6\]]la kha dog so sor bslab par bya/_/'byung ba lnga yi rlung zin pas ni du ba smig rgyu me khyer mar me sprin med nam mkha' 'byung /_/brtan pa'i rtags su zla zer nyi zer glog gi zer dang 'ja' tshon nyi zla bsres pa dngos su mthong /_/spyod lam dang ni sbyor ba mkhas pas dug sogs gzhom
[\[87a.7\]]dang 'chi ba brtag par sna tshogs bsgyur/_/rtsa dang rlung dang thig le 'dres pas bde gsal mi rtog rgyun mi 'chad pa'i rgyal por 'gyur ro kye/_/rim pa 'di nyid 'phel bar bya phyir snang dmigs dngos po sgyu mar bsams la dben pa'i gnas su ni/_/rdo rje sems dpa' mtshan

[\[87b.1\]]dpes spras pa'i gzugs brnyan la ni rab tu dmigs la dngos po chu zla ltar/_/bcu gnyis sgyu ma'i dpe yis mtshon te mnyam rjes la ni chos brgyad las 'das mkha' bzhin snyoms par 'gyur/_/de ltar shes pas mi bya ba med sngags zlos srung sogs mi dgos dge slong sogs

[\[87b.5\]]cig skyes sogs rtsa bsnyen bya/_/cig car mgon po bsgoms nas mtha' gnas rdo rje'i bzlas pa rtsa la mkhas pas pad+ma'i skyon bzhi bsal/_/bde ba'i lam drang ye shes mtshon pa mar me 'du ba rgyu 'bras shes nas shes bya'i dkyil 'khor blta/_/thur sel bcud nas glang

[\[88a.1\]]ye shes lus can sgra brnyan lta bu bral/_/mig sogs stong dang bdud bzhi grol ba chos nyid la mkhas gsum pa gcig gyur ye shes rgyun chad med/_/gzhi lam 'bras bu gcig gyur bde chen dngos po ro mnyam yi ge bzhi don 'bras bu mngon du 'gyur/_/mthar

[\[160b.1\]]dngos grub nyid du shes par bya zhes dgongs so/_/ji skad du/_/'jug pa yis ni spyan drangs te/_/myur ba yis ni gshegs su gsol/_/gnas pa yis ni bzhugs su gsol/_/rnam bzhi bla med dngos grub bo/_/zhes 'byung ngo /_/slar yang bshad pa/_spyan drangs pa zhes bya ba la/_
[\[160b.2\]]rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma bskul ba'o/_/gshegs su gsol zhes bya ba ni/_/'jig rten gyi khams mtha' yas su spro ba'o/_/bzhugs su gsol ba zhes bya ba ni/_spu ri'i yi ge la 'jug pa ste/_rab tu gnas par shes par bya'o/_/rang rig tsam du ngal so pa ni bla na med pa'i dngos grub bo/_/
[\[160b.3\]]gsang ba'i bshad pa ni/_spyan drangs ba zhes bya ba la shes rab la 'khyud pa'o/_/gshegs su gsol ba zhes bya ba ni/_dga' bral gyi gnas skabs su sangs rgyas kyi gzugs su spro ba'o/_/de'i gong bu thig le 'dzin pa ni rab tu gnas par shes par bya'o/_/dpe lhan cig skyes pa grub
[\[160b.4\]]pa ni rab tu gnas pa'i 'bras bu rtogs par bya'o/_/yang bshad pa spyan drangs pa zhes bya ba ni/_'dod chags chen po'i ting nge 'dzin la gnas te/_'dod chags thams cad dgug pa'o/_/gshegs su gsol ba zhes bya ba ni de bzhin gshegs pa dang lha mo dang khro bo'i gzugs su spro
[\[160b.5\]]ba'o/_/gshegs su gsol ba zhes bya ba ni/_khu ba'i thig le'i ngo bo nyid du bsams pa ni rab tu gnas pa shes par bya'o/_/de la gshegs su gsol ba ni bzhugs su gsol ba'i go rims bzlog nas shes par bya'o/_/spyan drangs ma thag par rab tu gnas pa'i phyir ro/_/des na gshegs
[\[160b.6\]]su gsol ba'i rjes la yang lha mo dang khro bo'i gzugs kyis sems can thams cad kyi re ba sna tshogs yongs su skong ba ni rab tu gnas pa'i 'bras bur shes par bya'o/_/bsnyen sgrub kyi yan lag bzhi po yang nang gi don du bshad par bya ste/_/bsnyen pa zhes bya ba ni/_/tshig snyan pa rnams

[\[161a.4\]]pa/_/rjes su mthun zhing g.yo sgyu med/_/bsnyen pa'i tshig gis ma nyes byas pa/_/yongs su brtsams dang a d+har myang /_/de la sogs pa'i las rnams kyis/_/rig ma dben par mnyes byas te/_/de nas yid 'byung sad par bya/_/mdzub mo gung mos mnan byas te/_/btsir zhing lte

[\[224a.4\]]bshams pa ni sha lnga dang bdud rtsi lnga dang dam tshig gi rdzas bdud rtsi ril bu dang gzhan yang zhal zas kyi khyad par rnam pa sna tshogs pa dang bza' ba dang btung ba la sogs pa'i longs spyod bya ba rnams bshams la ras dmar pos g.yogs la gzhag go/_/der dang por rnal 'byor pho mo thams
[\[224a.5\]]cad khrus byas te/_bdud rtsi lnga dang dri bzang pos lus byugs te/_gos sar pa dang /_rus pa la sogs pa'i rgyan dang /_mgo la me tog bzhag pa'am/_phreng ba bcings te thig btab pa'i le'u tshe'am/_pho mos spel ba rang rang gi gnas su 'dug ste/_rje btsun ma'i rnal 'byor

[\[249a.7\]]DA ki nI ye/_badzra war+NA nI ye hUM hUM hUM phaT phaT phaT swA hA/_nye ba'i snying po'i sngags so/_/dpal u rgyan rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i gnas nas rnam par byung ba rdo rje phag mo'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so//_//bod kyi lo tsA ba ban+de mar ba chos kyi dbang phyug nyid kyis bsgyur ba'o//_//
